--><!-- react-empty: 1472 --></div></div><div class="List-item"><div class="ContentItem AnswerItem" data-za-index="10" data-zop="{&quot;authorName&quot;:&quot;小小造数君&quot;,&quot;itemId&quot;:172891401,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;Python 的练手项目有哪些值得推荐？&quot;,&quot;type&quot;:&quot;answer&quot;}" name="172891401" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemtype="http://schema.org/Answer" itemscope="" data-za-module="AnswerItem" data-za-module-info="{&quot;card&quot;:{&quot;has_image&quot;:false,&quot;has_video&quot;:false,&quot;content&quot;:{&quot;type&quot;:&quot;Answer&quot;,&quot;token&quot;:&quot;172891401&quot;,&quot;upvote_num&quot;:252,&quot;comment_num&quot;:17,&quot;publish_timestamp&quot;:null,&quot;parent_token&quot;:&quot;29372574&quot;,&quot;author_member_hash_id&quot;:&quot;448581d57e7ff92b49b3fbad31905efe&quot;}}}"><div class="ContentItem-meta"><div class="AnswerItem-meta AnswerItem-meta--related"><div class="AuthorInfo" itemprop="author" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person"><meta itemprop="name" content="小小造数君"><meta itemprop="image" content="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-68efd76f0f36fdf9bd04f9e9e4143fe8_hd.jpg"><meta itemprop="url" content="https://www.zhihu.com/people/zao-xiao-shu"><meta itemprop="zhihu:followerCount" content="3057"><span class="UserLink AuthorInfo-avatarWrapper"><div class="Popover"><div id="Popover-38925-41304-toggle" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false" aria-owns="Popover-38925-41304-content"><a class="UserLink-link" data-za-detail-view-element_name="User" href="/people/zao-xiao-shu"><img class="Avatar AuthorInfo-avatar" width="38" height="38" src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-68efd76f0f36fdf9bd04f9e9e4143fe8_xs.jpg" srcset="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-68efd76f0f36fdf9bd04f9e9e4143fe8_l.jpg 2x" alt="小小造数君"></a></div><!-- react-empty: 1487 --></div></span><div class="AuthorInfo-content"><div class="AuthorInfo-head"><span class="UserLink AuthorInfo-name"><div class="Popover"><div id="Popover-38925-99147-toggle" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false" aria-owns="Popover-38925-99147-content"><a class="UserLink-link" data-za-detail-view-element_name="User" href="/people/zao-xiao-shu">小小造数君</a></div><!-- react-empty: 1494 --></div></span></div><div class="AuthorInfo-detail"><div class="AuthorInfo-badge"><!-- react-empty: 1497 --></div></div></div></div><div class="AnswerItem-extraInfo"><span class="Voters"><button class="Button Button--plain" type="button"><!-- react-text: 1501 -->252 人赞同了该回答<!-- /react-text --></button><!-- react-empty: 1502 --></span></div></div></div><meta itemprop="image" content="https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b4dfd95f62c428e9bc65378bf70f9d4e_200x112.jpg"><meta itemprop="upvoteCount" content="252"><meta itemprop="url" content="https://www.zhihu.com/question/29372574/answer/172891401"><meta itemprop="dateCreated" content="2017-05-22T05:23:01.000Z"><meta itemprop="dateModified" content="2017-05-22T05:23:01.000Z"><meta itemprop="commentCount" content="17"><div class="RichContent RichContent--unescapable"><div class="RichContent-inner"><span class="RichText CopyrightRichText-richText" itemprop="text"><a href="https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//www.zaoshu.io/%3Futm_source%3Dzhihu%26utm_campaign%3DGetcode%26utm_medium%3Dzhihuzaoshu" class=" wrap external" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer">造数 - 这次带你扒一扒 知乎日报<i class="icon-external"></i></a><p><b>1、获取源码</b></p><div class="highlight"><pre><code class="language-python"><span></span> <span class="kn">import</span> <span class="nn">requests</span>

<span class="n">url</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="s1">'http://daily.zhihu.com/'</span>
<span class="n">res</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">requests</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">get</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">url</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">text</span>
<span class="k">print</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">res</span><span class="p">)</span>
</code></pre></div><p>  个人喜欢requests，直接访问，发现返回500错误</p><div class="highlight"><pre><code class="language-python"><span></span><span class="n">C</span><span class="p">:</span>\<span class="n">Python35</span>\<span class="n">python</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">exe</span> <span class="n">F</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="o">/</span><span class="n">PyCharm</span><span class="o">/</span><span class="err">爬虫</span><span class="o">/</span><span class="n">daily</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">py</span>
<span class="o">&lt;</span><span class="n">html</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;</span><span class="n">body</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;</span><span class="n">h1</span><span class="o">&gt;</span><span class="mi">500</span> <span class="n">Server</span> <span class="n">Error</span><span class="o">&lt;/</span><span class="n">h1</span><span class="o">&gt;</span>
<span class="n">An</span> <span class="n">internal</span> <span class="n">server</span> <span class="n">error</span> <span class="n">occured</span><span class="o">.</span>
<span class="o">&lt;/</span><span class="n">body</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;/</span><span class="n">html</span><span class="o">&gt;</span>


<span class="n">Process</span> <span class="n">finished</span> <span class="k">with</span> <span class="nb">exit</span> <span class="n">code</span> <span class="mi">0</span>
</code></pre></div><p>  根据经验判断，是知乎禁止爬虫，需要加上一些伪装，让我们看看加上浏览器伪装效果</p><div class="highlight"><pre><code class="language-text"><span></span>import requests

headers = {'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 6.1; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/58.0.3029.110 Safari/537.36'}
url = 'http://daily.zhihu.com/'
res = requests.get(url,headers=headers).text
print(res)
</code></pre></div><p>  看看结果，已经返回我们需要的数据</p><div class="highlight"><pre><code class="language-python"><span></span>  <span class="n">C</span><span class="p">:</span>\<span class="n">Python35</span>\<span class="n">python</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">exe</span> <span class="n">F</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="o">/</span><span class="n">PyCharm</span><span class="o">/</span><span class="err">爬虫</span><span class="o">/</span><span class="n">daily</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">py</span>
<span class="o">&lt;</span><span class="err">!</span><span class="n">DOCTYPE</span> <span class="n">html</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;</span><span class="n">html</span> <span class="n">lang</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"zh-CN"</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;</span><span class="n">head</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;</span><span class="n">title</span><span class="o">&gt;</span><span class="err">知乎日报</span> <span class="o">-</span> <span class="err">每天</span> <span class="mi">3</span> <span class="err">次，每次</span> <span class="mi">7</span> <span class="err">分钟</span><span class="o">&lt;/</span><span class="n">title</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;</span><span class="n">meta</span> <span class="n">charset</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"utf-8"</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;</span><span class="n">meta</span> <span class="n">http</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="n">equiv</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"X-UA-Compatible"</span> <span class="n">content</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"IE=edge,chrome=1"</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;</span><span class="n">meta</span> <span class="n">name</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"description"</span> <span class="n">content</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"在中国，资讯类移动应用的人均阅读时长是 5 分钟，而在知乎日报，这个数字是 21。以独有的方式为你提供最高质、最深度、最有收获的阅读体验。"</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;</span><span class="n">link</span> <span class="n">rel</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"stylesheet"</span> <span class="n">href</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"/css/base.auto.css"</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;</span><span class="n">link</span> <span class="n">rel</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"stylesheet"</span> <span class="n">href</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"/css/new_home_v3.auto.css"</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;</span><span class="n">script</span> <span class="n">src</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"/js/jquery.1.9.1.js"</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;/</span><span class="n">script</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;</span><span class="n">script</span> <span class="n">src</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"/js/new_index_v3/home.js"</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;/</span><span class="n">script</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;</span><span class="n">link</span> <span class="n">rel</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"shortcut icon"</span> <span class="n">href</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"/favicon.ico"</span> <span class="nb">type</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"image/x-icon"</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;</span><span class="n">base</span> <span class="n">target</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"_blank"</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;</span><span class="n">style</span><span class="o">&gt;</span><span class="n">h1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="n">h2</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="n">h3</span> <span class="p">{</span><span class="n">padding</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">;</span><span class="n">margin</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">}</span><span class="o">&lt;/</span><span class="n">style</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;</span><span class="n">base</span> <span class="n">target</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"_blank"</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;/</span><span class="n">head</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;</span><span class="n">body</span> <span class="n">class</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"home"</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;</span><span class="n">a</span> <span class="n">href</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"javascript:;"</span> <span class="n">title</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"回到顶部"</span> <span class="n">class</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"back-to-top"</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;/</span><span class="n">a</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;</span><span class="n">div</span> <span class="n">class</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"header navbar-fixed-top"</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;</span><span class="n">div</span> <span class="n">class</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"container-fixed-width clearfix"</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;</span><span class="n">div</span> <span class="n">class</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"top-nav-link"</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;</span><span class="n">a</span> <span class="n">href</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"javascript:;"</span> <span class="n">data</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="n">offset</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"470"</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;</span><span class="n">span</span><span class="o">&gt;</span><span class="err">浏览内容</span><span class="o">&lt;/</span><span class="n">span</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;/</span><span class="n">a</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;</span><span class="n">a</span> <span class="n">href</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"javascript:;"</span> <span class="n">data</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="n">offset</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"0"</span> <span class="n">class</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"active"</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;</span><span class="n">span</span><span class="o">&gt;</span><span class="n">App</span> <span class="err">下载</span><span class="o">&lt;/</span><span class="n">span</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;/</span><span class="n">a</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;/</span><span class="n">div</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;</span><span class="n">h1</span> <span class="n">class</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"logo"</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;</span><span class="n">a</span> <span class="n">href</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"http://daily.zhihu.com/"</span> <span class="n">title</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"知乎日报"</span> <span class="n">class</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"link-logo"</span><span class="o">&gt;</span><span class="err">知乎日报</span><span class="o">&lt;/</span><span class="n">a</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;/</span><span class="n">h1</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;/</span><span class="n">div</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;/</span><span class="n">div</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;</span><span class="n">div</span> <span class="n">class</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"download"</span><span class="o">&gt;</span>
<span class="o">...</span>
</code></pre></div><p>  但是这种写法是否可以应用到所有的网站?</p><p>  答案是“不”</p><br><figure><noscript>&lt;img src="https://pic3.zhimg.com/50/v2-b4dfd95f62c428e9bc65378bf70f9d4e_hd.png" data-rawwidth="500" data-rawheight="500" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="500" data-original="https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b4dfd95f62c428e9bc65378bf70f9d4e_r.png"&gt;</noscript><span><div data-reactroot="" class="VagueImage origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" data-src="https://pic3.zhimg.com/50/v2-b4dfd95f62c428e9bc65378bf70f9d4e_hd.jpg" style="width: 500px; height: 500px;"><div class="VagueImage-mask is-active"></div></div></span></figure><p><b>2、代理设置</b></p><p>有时候同一个IP去爬取同一网站上的内容，久了之后就会被该网站服务器屏蔽。解决方法就是更换IP。这个时候，在对方网站上，显示的不是我们真实地IP地址，而是代理服务器的IP地址。</p><p><a href="https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xicidaili.com/nn/" class=" external" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer"><span class="invisible">http://www.</span><span class="visible">xicidaili.com/nn/</span><span class="invisible"></span><i class="icon-external"></i></a> 西刺代理提供了很多可用的国内IP，可以直接拿来使用。</p><br><figure><noscript>&lt;img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-89bbe2447c1b424aa37ca6a68e9e4dbc_hd.png" data-rawwidth="1109" data-rawheight="702" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1109" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-89bbe2447c1b424aa37ca6a68e9e4dbc_r.png"&gt;</noscript><span><div data-reactroot="" class="VagueImage origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" data-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-89bbe2447c1b424aa37ca6a68e9e4dbc_hd.jpg" style="width: 654px; height: 413.984px;"><div class="VagueImage-mask is-active"></div></div></span></figure><p>那么如何在爬虫里加入代理呢，看看requests的官方文档怎么说。<a href="https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//docs.python-requests.org/zh_CN/latest/user/advanced.html%23proxies" class=" external" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer"><span class="invisible">http://</span><span class="visible">docs.python-requests.org</span><span class="invisible">/zh_CN/latest/user/advanced.html#proxies</span><span class="ellipsis"></span><i class="icon-external"></i></a></p><p>如果需要使用代理，你可以通过为任意请求方法提供 proxies 参数来配置单个请求:</p><div class="highlight"><pre><code class="language-python"><span></span><span class="kn">import</span> <span class="nn">requests</span>

<span class="n">proxies</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">{</span>
  <span class="s2">"http"</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="s2">"http://10.10.1.10:3128"</span><span class="p">,</span>
  <span class="s2">"https"</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="s2">"http://10.10.1.10:1080"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="p">}</span>

<span class="n">requests</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">get</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s2">"http://example.org"</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">proxies</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">proxies</span><span class="p">)</span>
</code></pre></div><p> 用法很简单，加入proxies参数即可 import requests</p><div class="highlight"><pre><code class="language-python"><span></span><span class="n">proxies</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">{</span>
  <span class="s2">"http"</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="s2">"http://121.201.24.248：8088"</span><span class="p">,</span>
  <span class="s2">"https"</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="s2">"http://36.249.194.52：8118"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
<span class="n">headers</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">{</span><span class="s1">'User-Agent'</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="s1">'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 6.1; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/58.0.3029.110 Safari/537.36'</span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="n">url</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="s1">'http://daily.zhihu.com/'</span>
<span class="n">res</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">requests</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">get</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">url</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="n">headers</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">headers</span><span class="err">，</span><span class="n">proxies</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">proxies</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">text</span>
<span class="k">print</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nb">len</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">res</span><span class="p">))</span>
</code></pre></div><p>为了便于测试，只打印出返回数据的长度</p><br><div class="highlight"><pre><code class="language-python"><span></span><span class="n">C</span><span class="p">:</span>\<span class="n">Python35</span>\<span class="n">python</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">exe</span> <span class="n">F</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="o">/</span><span class="n">PyCharm</span><span class="o">/</span><span class="err">爬虫</span><span class="o">/</span><span class="n">daily</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">py</span>
<span class="mi">10830</span>

<span class="n">Process</span> <span class="n">finished</span> <span class="k">with</span> <span class="nb">exit</span> <span class="n">code</span> <span class="mi">0</span>
</code></pre></div><p>  发现代理服务器成功爬取知乎日报的信息，内容是10830，故意把代理IP写错一位数，看看结果</p><div class="highlight"><pre><code class="language-python"><span></span>   <span class="kn">import</span> <span class="nn">requests</span>

<span class="n">proxies</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">{</span>
  <span class="s2">"http"</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="s2">"http://121.201.24.248：8088"</span><span class="p">,</span>
  <span class="s2">"https"</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="s2">"http://36.249.194.52: 222"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
<span class="n">headers</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">{</span><span class="s1">'User-Agent'</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="s1">'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 6.1; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/58.0.3029.110 Safari/537.36'</span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="n">url</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="s1">'http://daily.zhihu.com/'</span>
<span class="n">res</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">requests</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">get</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">url</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="n">headers</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">headers</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="n">proxies</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">proxies</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">text</span>
<span class="k">print</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nb">len</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">res</span><span class="p">))</span>
</code></pre></div><p>我们把"https": "<a href="https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//36.249.194.52" class=" external" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer"><span class="invisible">http://</span><span class="visible">36.249.194.52</span><span class="invisible"></span><i class="icon-external"></i></a>：8118"修改为"https": "<a href="https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//36.249.194.52" class=" external" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer"><span class="invisible">http://</span><span class="visible">36.249.194.52</span><span class="invisible"></span><i class="icon-external"></i></a>: 222"，此时返回的结果如下，发现不能获取网页数据。所以，在使用代理服务器爬去网站时，如果出现异常，要考虑代理IP是否失效了。 当然你也可以写一个爬虫，实时抓取最新的代理IP用来爬取。</p><div class="highlight"><pre><code class="language-python"><span></span><span class="n">Traceback</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">most</span> <span class="n">recent</span> <span class="n">call</span> <span class="n">last</span><span class="p">):</span>
  <span class="n">File</span> <span class="s2">"F:/PyCharm/爬虫/daily.py"</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">line</span> <span class="mi">9</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="ow">in</span> <span class="o">&lt;</span><span class="n">module</span><span class="o">&gt;</span>
    <span class="n">res</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">requests</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">get</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">url</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="n">headers</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">headers</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="n">proxies</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">proxies</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">text</span>
  <span class="n">File</span> <span class="s2">"C:\Python35\lib\site-packages</span><span class="se">\r</span><span class="s2">equests</span><span class="se">\a</span><span class="s2">pi.py"</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">line</span> <span class="mi">70</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="ow">in</span> <span class="n">get</span>
    <span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">request</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s1">'get'</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">url</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">params</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">params</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="o">**</span><span class="n">kwargs</span><span class="p">)</span>
  <span class="n">File</span> <span class="s2">"C:\Python35\lib\site-packages</span><span class="se">\r</span><span class="s2">equests</span><span class="se">\a</span><span class="s2">pi.py"</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">line</span> <span class="mi">56</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="ow">in</span> <span class="n">request</span>
    <span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">session</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">request</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">method</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">method</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">url</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">url</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="o">**</span><span class="n">kwargs</span><span class="p">)</span>
  <span class="n">File</span> <span class="s2">"C:\Python35\lib\site-packages</span><span class="se">\r</span><span class="s2">equests\sessions.py"</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">line</span> <span class="mi">488</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="ow">in</span> <span class="n">request</span>
    <span class="n">resp</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">send</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">prep</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="o">**</span><span class="n">send_kwargs</span><span class="p">)</span>
  <span class="n">File</span> <span class="s2">"C:\Python35\lib\site-packages</span><span class="se">\r</span><span class="s2">equests\sessions.py"</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">line</span> <span class="mi">609</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="ow">in</span> <span class="n">send</span>
    <span class="n">r</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">adapter</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">send</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">request</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="o">**</span><span class="n">kwargs</span><span class="p">)</span>
  <span class="n">File</span> <span class="s2">"C:\Python35\lib\site-packages</span><span class="se">\r</span><span class="s2">equests</span><span class="se">\a</span><span class="s2">dapters.py"</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">line</span> <span class="mi">485</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="ow">in</span> <span class="n">send</span>
    <span class="k">raise</span> <span class="n">ProxyError</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">e</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">request</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">request</span><span class="p">)</span>
<span class="n">requests</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">exceptions</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">ProxyError</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">HTTPConnectionPool</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">host</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s1">'121.201.24.248：8088'</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">port</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="mi">80</span><span class="p">):</span> <span class="n">Max</span> <span class="n">retries</span> <span class="n">exceeded</span> <span class="k">with</span> <span class="n">url</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">http</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="o">//</span><span class="n">daily</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">zhihu</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">com</span><span class="o">/</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">Caused</span> <span class="n">by</span> <span class="n">ProxyError</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s1">'Cannot connect to proxy.'</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">NewConnectionError</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s1">'&lt;requests.packages.urllib3.connection.HTTPConnection object at 0x0000000003860DA0&gt;: Failed to establish a new connection: [Errno 11004] getaddrinfo failed'</span><span class="p">,)))</span>
</code></pre></div><p><b>3、模拟登录</b></p><p>有些网站是需要登录才能看到信息的，例如知乎，直接用requests获取知乎首页信息，返回数据是需要你登录的，只有登录了才能看到数据。</p><div class="highlight"><pre><code class="language-python"><span></span><span class="o">&lt;</span><span class="n">button</span> <span class="nb">type</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"button"</span> <span class="n">class</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"signin-switch-button"</span><span class="o">&gt;</span><span class="err">手机验证码登录</span><span class="o">&lt;/</span><span class="n">button</span><span class="o">&gt;</span>

<span class="o">&lt;</span><span class="n">a</span> <span class="n">class</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"unable-login"</span> <span class="n">href</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"#"</span><span class="o">&gt;</span><span class="err">无法登录？</span><span class="o">&lt;/</span><span class="n">a</span><span class="o">&gt;</span>
<span class="o">&lt;/</span><span class="n">div</span><span class="o">&gt;</span>

<span class="o">&lt;</span><span class="n">div</span> <span class="n">class</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"social-signup-wrapper"</span> <span class="n">data</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="n">za</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="n">module</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"SNSSignIn"</span><span class="o">&gt;</span>
<span class="o">&lt;</span><span class="n">span</span> <span class="n">class</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"name js-toggle-sns-buttons"</span><span class="o">&gt;</span><span class="err">社交帐号登录</span><span class="o">&lt;/</span><span class="n">span</span><span class="o">&gt;</span>

<span class="o">&lt;</span><span class="n">div</span> <span class="n">class</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"sns-buttons"</span><span class="o">&gt;</span>
<span class="o">&lt;</span><span class="n">a</span> <span class="n">title</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"微信登录"</span> <span class="n">class</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"js-bindwechat"</span> <span class="n">href</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"#"</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;</span><span class="n">i</span> <span class="n">class</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"sprite-index-icon-wechat"</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;/</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;/</span><span class="n">a</span><span class="o">&gt;</span>
<span class="o">&lt;</span><span class="n">a</span> <span class="n">title</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"微博登录"</span> <span class="n">class</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"js-bindweibo"</span> <span class="n">href</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"#"</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;</span><span class="n">i</span> <span class="n">class</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"sprite-index-icon-weibo"</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;/</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;/</span><span class="n">a</span><span class="o">&gt;</span>
<span class="o">&lt;</span><span class="n">a</span> <span class="n">title</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"QQ 登录"</span> <span class="n">class</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"js-bindqq"</span> <span class="n">href</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"#"</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;</span><span class="n">i</span> <span class="n">class</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">"sprite-index-icon-qq"</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;/</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="o">&gt;&lt;/</span><span class="n">a</span><span class="o">&gt;</span>
<span class="o">&lt;/</span><span class="n">div</span><span class="o">&gt;</span>
</code></pre></div><p>再次回到官方文档<a href="https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//docs.python-requests.org/zh_CN/latest/user/quickstart.html%23cookie" class=" external" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer"><span class="invisible">http://</span><span class="visible">docs.python-requests.org</span><span class="invisible">/zh_CN/latest/user/quickstart.html#cookie</span><span class="ellipsis"></span><i class="icon-external"></i></a></p><div class="highlight"><pre><code class="language-python"><span></span><span class="err">如果某个响应中包含一些</span> <span class="n">cookie</span><span class="err">，你可以快速访问它们：</span>

<span class="o">&gt;&gt;&gt;</span> <span class="n">url</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="s1">'http://example.com/some/cookie/setting/url'</span>
<span class="o">&gt;&gt;&gt;</span> <span class="n">r</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">requests</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">get</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">url</span><span class="p">)</span>

<span class="o">&gt;&gt;&gt;</span> <span class="n">r</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">cookies</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="s1">'example_cookie_name'</span><span class="p">]</span>
<span class="s1">'example_cookie_value'</span>
<span class="err">要想发送你的</span><span class="n">cookies</span><span class="err">到服务器，可以使用</span> <span class="n">cookies</span> <span class="err">参数：</span>

<span class="o">&gt;&gt;&gt;</span> <span class="n">url</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="s1">'http://httpbin.org/cookies'</span>
<span class="o">&gt;&gt;&gt;</span> <span class="n">cookies</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="nb">dict</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">cookies_are</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s1">'working'</span><span class="p">)</span>

<span class="o">&gt;&gt;&gt;</span> <span class="n">r</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">requests</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">get</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">url</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">cookies</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">cookies</span><span class="p">)</span>
<span class="o">&gt;&gt;&gt;</span> <span class="n">r</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">text</span>
<span class="s1">'{"cookies": {"cookies_are": "working"}}'</span>

</code></pre></div><p>具体的分析过程可以参考xchaoinfo所写的文章和视频，讲解十分清晰<a href="https://zhuanlan.zhihu.com/p/25633789" class="internal"><span class="invisible">https://</span><span class="visible">zhuanlan.zhihu.com/p/25</span><span class="invisible">633789</span><span class="ellipsis"></span></a> 下面是代码</p><div class="highlight"><pre><code class="language-python"><span></span>    <span class="kn">import</span> <span class="nn">requests</span>
<span class="kn">from</span> <span class="nn">bs4</span> <span class="kn">import</span> <span class="n">BeautifulSoup</span>
<span class="kn">import</span> <span class="nn">os</span><span class="o">,</span> <span class="nn">time</span>
<span class="kn">import</span> <span class="nn">re</span>
<span class="c1"># import http.cookiejar as cookielib</span>

<span class="c1"># 构造 Request headers</span>
<span class="n">agent</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="s1">'Mozilla/5.0 (Linux; Android 6.0; Nexus 5 Build/MRA58N) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/56.0.2924.87 Mobile Safari/537.36'</span>
<span class="n">headers</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">{</span>
    <span class="s2">"Host"</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="s2">"www.zhihu.com"</span><span class="p">,</span>
    <span class="s2">"Referer"</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="s2">"https://www.zhihu.com/"</span><span class="p">,</span>
    <span class="s1">'User-Agent'</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">agent</span>
<span class="p">}</span>

<span class="c1">######### 构造用于网络请求的session</span>
<span class="n">session</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">requests</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">Session</span><span class="p">()</span>
<span class="c1"># session.cookies = cookielib.LWPCookieJar(filename='zhihucookie')</span>
<span class="c1"># try:</span>
<span class="c1">#     session.cookies.load(ignore_discard=True)</span>
<span class="c1"># except:</span>
<span class="c1">#     print('cookie 文件未能加载')</span>

<span class="c1">############ 获取xsrf_token</span>
<span class="n">homeurl</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="s1">'https://www.zhihu.com'</span>
<span class="n">homeresponse</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">session</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">get</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">url</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">homeurl</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">headers</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">headers</span><span class="p">)</span>
<span class="n">homesoup</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">BeautifulSoup</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">homeresponse</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">text</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="s1">'html.parser'</span><span class="p">)</span>
<span class="n">xsrfinput</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">homesoup</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">find</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s1">'input'</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="p">{</span><span class="s1">'name'</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="s1">'_xsrf'</span><span class="p">})</span>
<span class="n">xsrf_token</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">xsrfinput</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="s1">'value'</span><span class="p">]</span>
<span class="k">print</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s2">"获取到的xsrf_token为： "</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">xsrf_token</span><span class="p">)</span>

<span class="c1">########## 获取验证码文件</span>
<span class="n">randomtime</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="nb">str</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nb">int</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">time</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">time</span><span class="p">()</span> <span class="o">*</span> <span class="mi">1000</span><span class="p">))</span>
<span class="n">captchaurl</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="s1">'https://www.zhihu.com/captcha.gif?r='</span><span class="o">+</span>\
             <span class="n">randomtime</span><span class="o">+</span><span class="s2">"&amp;type=login"</span>
<span class="n">captcharesponse</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">session</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">get</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">url</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">captchaurl</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">headers</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">headers</span><span class="p">)</span>
<span class="k">with</span> <span class="nb">open</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s1">'checkcode.gif'</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="s1">'wb'</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="k">as</span> <span class="n">f</span><span class="p">:</span>
    <span class="n">f</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">write</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">captcharesponse</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">content</span><span class="p">)</span>
    <span class="n">f</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">close</span><span class="p">()</span>
<span class="c1"># os.startfile('checkcode.gif')</span>
<span class="n">captcha</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="nb">input</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s1">'请输入验证码：'</span><span class="p">)</span>
<span class="k">print</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">captcha</span><span class="p">)</span>

<span class="c1">########### 开始登陆</span>
<span class="n">headers</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="s1">'X-Xsrftoken'</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">xsrf_token</span>
<span class="n">headers</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="s1">'X-Requested-With'</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="s1">'XMLHttpRequest'</span>
<span class="n">loginurl</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="s1">'https://www.zhihu.com/login/email'</span>
<span class="n">postdata</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">{</span>
    <span class="s1">'_xsrf'</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">xsrf_token</span><span class="p">,</span>
    <span class="s1">'email'</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="s1">'邮箱@qq.com'</span><span class="p">,</span>
    <span class="s1">'password'</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="s1">'密码'</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
<span class="n">loginresponse</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">session</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">post</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">url</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">loginurl</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">headers</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">headers</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">data</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">postdata</span><span class="p">)</span>
<span class="k">print</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s1">'服务器端返回响应码：'</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">loginresponse</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">status_code</span><span class="p">)</span>
<span class="k">print</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">loginresponse</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">json</span><span class="p">())</span>
<span class="c1"># 验证码问题输入导致失败: 猜测这个问题是由于session中对于验证码的请求过期导致</span>
<span class="k">if</span> <span class="n">loginresponse</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">json</span><span class="p">()[</span><span class="s1">'r'</span><span class="p">]</span><span class="o">==</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">:</span>
    <span class="c1"># 重新输入验证码，再次运行代码则正常。也就是说可以再第一次不输入验证码，或者输入一个错误的验证码，只有第二次才是有效的</span>
    <span class="n">randomtime</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="nb">str</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nb">int</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">time</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">time</span><span class="p">()</span> <span class="o">*</span> <span class="mi">1000</span><span class="p">))</span>
    <span class="n">captchaurl</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="s1">'https://www.zhihu.com/captcha.gif?r='</span> <span class="o">+</span> \
                 <span class="n">randomtime</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="s2">"&amp;type=login"</span>
    <span class="n">captcharesponse</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">session</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">get</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">url</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">captchaurl</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">headers</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">headers</span><span class="p">)</span>
    <span class="k">with</span> <span class="nb">open</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s1">'checkcode.gif'</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="s1">'wb'</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="k">as</span> <span class="n">f</span><span class="p">:</span>
        <span class="n">f</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">write</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">captcharesponse</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">content</span><span class="p">)</span>
        <span class="n">f</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">close</span><span class="p">()</span>
    <span class="n">os</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">startfile</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s1">'checkcode.gif'</span><span class="p">)</span>
    <span class="n">captcha</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="nb">input</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s1">'请输入验证码：'</span><span class="p">)</span>
    <span class="k">print</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">captcha</span><span class="p">)</span>

    <span class="n">postdata</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="s1">'captcha'</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">captcha</span>
    <span class="n">loginresponse</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">session</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">post</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">url</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">loginurl</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">headers</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">headers</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">data</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">postdata</span><span class="p">)</span>
    <span class="k">print</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s1">'服务器端返回响应码：'</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">loginresponse</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">status_code</span><span class="p">)</span>
    <span class="k">print</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">loginresponse</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">json</span><span class="p">())</span>




<span class="c1">##########################保存登陆后的cookie信息</span>
<span class="c1"># session.cookies.save()</span>
<span class="c1">############################判断是否登录成功</span>
<span class="n">profileurl</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="s1">'https://www.zhihu.com/settings/profile'</span>
<span class="n">profileresponse</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">session</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">get</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">url</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">profileurl</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">headers</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">headers</span><span class="p">)</span>
<span class="k">print</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s1">'profile页面响应码：'</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">profileresponse</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">status_code</span><span class="p">)</span>
<span class="n">profilesoup</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">BeautifulSoup</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">profileresponse</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">text</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="s1">'html.parser'</span><span class="p">)</span>
<span class="n">div</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">profilesoup</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">find</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s1">'div'</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="p">{</span><span class="s1">'id'</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="s1">'rename-section'</span><span class="p">})</span>
<span class="k">print</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">div</span><span class="p">)</span>
</code></pre></div><br><p>好了关于爬虫的第一步，获取源码这一节讲了很多，其实大多数网站加上User-Agent和代理IP就可以正常爬取。下一节会讲讲如何利用xpath来解析网页，获取我们想要的数据。</p><p>p.s：本周二造数君的优秀同事小歪会在趣直播讲一讲Python爬虫入门，欢迎大家来参加。<a href="https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//m.quzhiboapp.com/%3FliveId%3D522%23%21/intro/522" class=" external" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer"><span class="invisible">http://</span><span class="visible">m.quzhiboapp.com/?</span><span class="invisible">liveId=522#!/intro/522</span><span class="ellipsis"></span><i class="icon-external"></i></a></p><br><p>最后一定要记得：</p><a class="RichContent-inner"><span class="RichText CopyrightRichText-richText" itemprop="text"><p>楼主要有挑战有意思的，建议<br>1.websocket 协议解析  锻炼socket编程，协议阅读，struct模块 估计行数600+</p><p>2.redis客户端实现，对你以后很有帮助</p><p>3.python sortedset实现，可使用redis的skiplist,用python封装 ，锻炼python c api</p>这都有点挑战，完成了会很有成就感，有很大提高</span><!-- react-empty: 2541 --></div><div><div class="ContentItem-time"><a target="_blank" href="/question/29372574/answer/53953499">发布于 2015-07-06</a></div><div class="AnswerReward"><!-- react-empty: 2899 --><!-- react-empty: 1620 --></div><button class="Button ContentItem-action Button--plain Button--withIcon Button--withLabel" type="button"><span style="display: inline-flex; align-items: center;"><!-- react-text: 2570 class="AnswerItem-extraInfo"><span class="Voters"><button class="Button Button--plain" type="button"><!-- react-text: 1908 -->77 人赞同了该回答<!-- /react-text --></button><!-- react-empty: 1909 --></span></div></div></div><meta itemprop="image" content=""><meta itemprop="upvoteCount" content="77"><meta itemprop="url" content="https://www.zhihu.com/question/29372574/answer/59717504"><meta itemprop="dateCreated" content="2015-08-18T03:45:07.000Z"><meta itemprop="dateModified" content="2015-08-18T03:45:07.000Z"><meta itemprop="commentCount" content="19"><div class="RichContent RichContent--unescapable"><div class="RichContent-inner"><span class="RichText CopyrightRichText-richText" itemprop="text">上面的回答，作为入门练手项目实在是太高大上了，我看了好惭愧。<br>python 哪里有这么不亲民。请大家和我一起高呼：知呼不装B，从我做起！<br>我刚学python时，做了以下几个工具类，都是为了方便自己：<br><ol><li>起点上自动下载txt小说的程序<br></li><li>公司考勤网站自动填写工时（一开始还做登录，后来发现他压根没用户校验，只管往对应url提交form就能接收，国内公司的安全真是..)<br></li><li>结合flex做了个知识库，记录自己的一些小心得</li></ol><p>另外运维工作，比如ssh自动登录、自动导入数据、迁移数据、格式化数据、自动设置编译等等小工具实在太多了。满足自己才是第一的。</p>当时的感觉，就像我自己掌握了门独门绝技，看着其他人努力的写java/c++ ，我用python轻松几行代码搞定，那叫一个酸爽。<br>这时不会满足当小工具用了，可以参与做一些开源项目了</span><!-- react-empty: 2637 --></div><div><div class="ContentItem-time"><a target="_blank" href="/question/29372574/answer/59717504">发布于 --><!-- react-empty: 2919 --><!-- react-empty: 2283 --></div></div><div class="List-item"><div class="ContentItem AnswerItem" data-za-index="18" data-zop="{&quot;authorName&quot;:&quot;林茜茜&quot;,&quot;itemId&quot;:86412439,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;Python 的练手项目有哪些值得推荐？&quot;,&quot;type&quot;:&quot;answer&quot;}" name="86412439" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemtype="http://schema.org/Answer" itemscope="" data-za-module="AnswerItem" data-za-module-info="{&quot;card&quot;:{&quot;has_image&quot;:false,&quot;has_video&quot;:false,&quot;content&quot;:{&quot;type&quot;:&quot;Answer&quot;,&quot;token&quot;:&quot;86412439&quot;,&quot;upvote_num&quot;:599,&quot;comment_num&quot;:58,&quot;publish_timestamp&quot;:null,&quot;parent_token&quot;:&quot;29372574&quot;,&quot;author_member_hash_id&quot;:&quot;960e5e06bd066473de06f7a00b6c80cc&quot;}}}"><div class="ContentItem-meta"><div class="AnswerItem-meta AnswerItem-meta--related"><div class="AuthorInfo" itemprop="author" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person"><meta itemprop="name" content="林茜茜"><meta itemprop="image" content="https://pic2.zhimg.com/50/fd9d946e1_hd.jpg"><meta itemprop="url" content="https://www.zhihu.com/people/lin-qian-qian"><meta itemprop="zhihu:followerCount" content="17470"><span class="UserLink AuthorInfo-avatarWrapper"><div class="Popover"><div id="Popover-38932-28764-toggle" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false" aria-owns="Popover-38932-28764-content"><a class="UserLink-link" data-za-detail-view-element_name="User" href="/people/lin-qian-qian"><img class="Avatar AuthorInfo-avatar" width="38" height="38" src="https://pic2.zhimg.com/50/fd9d946e1_xs.jpg" srcset="https://pic2.zhimg.com/50/fd9d946e1_l.jpg 2x" alt="林茜茜"></a></div><!-- react-empty: 2298 --></div></span><div class="AuthorInfo-content"><div class="AuthorInfo-head"><span class="UserLink AuthorInfo-name"><div class="Popover"><div id="Popover-38932-26208-toggle" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false" aria-owns="Popover-38932-26208-content"><a class="UserLink-link" data-za-detail-view-element_name="User" href="/people/lin-qian-qian">林茜茜</a></div><!-- react-empty: 2305 --></div></span></div><div class="AuthorInfo-detail"><div class="AuthorInfo-badge"><div class="RichText AuthorInfo-badgeText">做最好看的编程课</div></div></div></div></div><div class="AnswerItem-extraInfo"><span class="Voters"><button class="Button Button--plain" type="button"><!-- react-text: 2312 -->599 人赞同了该回答<!-- /react-text --></button><!-- react-empty: 2313 --></span></div></div></div><meta itemprop="image" content="https://pic4.zhimg.com/0ceeca4f258179e2744011e2ffda1d07_200x112.jpg"><meta itemprop="upvoteCount" content="599"><meta itemprop="url" content="https://www.zhihu.com/question/29372574/answer/86412439"><meta itemprop="dateCreated" content="2016-02-15T10:57:21.000Z"><meta itemprop="dateModified" content="2016-02-27T13:14:22.000Z"><meta itemprop="commentCount" content="58"><div class="RichContent RichContent--unescapable"><div class="RichContent-inner"><span class="RichText CopyrightRichText-richText" itemprop="text"><p>发现这个问题下面的大多数回答都不适合初学者。找不到好的练手项目可能是新手最头疼的问题。</p><p>明明知道，只有动手做点东西出来，才能真正学会编程。</p><p>然而，很难找到适合学习的编程项目。Github 源码，看不懂。九九乘法表之类的项目，太无聊。跟着视频课程敲一遍，等到自己写的时候还是不会。</p><p>为了解救大部分新手的这个问题，为你们量身定制了一个综合的爬虫系统实战项目：爬取10w 以上的二手商品数据存储在 MongoDB中，进行数据统计，然后用 Django 网站展示二手商品行情。</p><p></p><figure><noscript>&amp;lt;img src="https://pic4.zhimg.com/50/0ceeca4f258179e2744011e2ffda1d07_hd.png" data-rawwidth="600" data-rawheight="369" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="600" data-original="https://pic4.zhimg.com/0ceeca4f258179e2744011e2ffda1d07_r.png"&amp;gt;</noscript><span><div data-reactroot="" class="VagueImage origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" data-src="https://pic4.zhimg.com/50/0ceeca4f258179e2744011e2ffda1d07_hd.jpg" style="width: 600px; height: 369px;"><div class="VagueImage-mask is-active"></div></div></span></figure><p></p><p>项目覆盖的技能点比较广，又有爬虫、又有 MongoDB、又有 Django，从后端写到前端。所以把这个大的项目拆解成了4个小的目标，让新手也能由浅入深的完成。</p><br><p>▋<b>目标1：学会爬取大多数网页</b></p><p></p><figure><noscript>&amp;lt;img src="https://pic4.zhimg.com/50/01ba5ce0ae09d18d53d23aa9bc0aced3_hd.png" data-rawwidth="600" data-rawheight="368" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="600" data-original="https://pic4.zhimg.com/01ba5ce0ae09d18d53d23aa9bc0aced3_r.png"&amp;gt;</noscript><span><div data-reactroot="" class="VagueImage origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" data-src="https://pic4.zhimg.com/50/01ba5ce0ae09d18d53d23aa9bc0aced3_hd.jpg" style="width: 600px; height: 368px;"><div class="VagueImage-mask is-active"></div></div></span></figure><p></p><p>很多人学 Python 就是为了做爬虫吧，直接爬取第一手信息，还是很实用的技能。</p><br><p>▋<b>目标2：学会爬取10w 以上的大规模数据</b></p><p></p><figure><noscript>&amp;lt;img src="https://pic4.zhimg.com/50/db3639627a347d0cb9ce1381b6cf2623_hd.png" data-rawwidth="600" data-rawheight="396" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="600" data-original="https://pic4.zhimg.com/db3639627a347d0cb9ce1381b6cf2623_r.png"&amp;gt;</noscript><span><div data-reactroot="" class="VagueImage origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" data-src="https://pic4.zhimg.com/50/db3639627a347d0cb9ce1381b6cf2623_hd.jpg" style="width: 600px; height: 396px;"><div class="VagueImage-mask is-active"></div></div></span></figure><p></p><p>每秒钟爬取下来成百上千的数据，在屏幕上快速滚动着。这时候最适合在同学面前装逼了。</p><p>▋<b>目标3：学会使用 MongoDB 对数据进行统计与分析</b></p><p></p><figure><noscript>&amp;lt;img src="https://pic4.zhimg.com/50/004472c536204840e0f74be3bb07c1cb_hd.png" data-rawwidth="600" data-rawheight="409" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="600" data-original="https://pic4.zhimg.com/004472c536204840e0f74be3bb07c1cb_r.png"&amp;gt;</noscript><span><div data-reactroot="" class="VagueImage origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" data-src="https://pic4.zhimg.com/50/004472c536204840e0f74be3bb07c1cb_hd.jpg" style="width: 600px; height: 409px;"><div class="VagueImage-mask is-active"></div></div></span></figure><p></p><p>仅仅是大量数据没有意义，还需要挖掘出来数据背后的意义。哪一类二手商品卖的最多？什么价格出手最合适？</p><p>▋<b>目标4：使用 Django 和 Semantic UI 框架搭建数据可视化的网页</b></p><br><p></p><figure><noscript>&amp;lt;img src="https://pic3.zhimg.com/50/d5392f5c331db8f0c4b0e862a592ac6e_hd.png" data-rawwidth="600" data-rawheight="374" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="600" data-original="https://pic3.zhimg.com/d5392f5c331db8f0c4b0e862a592ac6e_r.png"&amp;gt;</noscript><span><div data-reactroot="" class="VagueImage origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" data-src="https://pic3.zhimg.com/50/d5392f5c331db8f0c4b0e862a592ac6e_hd.jpg" style="width: 600px; height: 374px;"><div class="VagueImage-mask is-active"></div></div></span></figure><p></p><p>把前面获得的成果进行数据可视化，在网页上展示出来。</p><p>你可能会问，基础薄弱的话，能学会么？</p><p>为了让新手能完成这个实战项目，我们把每个目标又拆分成了3个阶段：理解 &gt; 模仿 &gt; 实战。</p><p></p><figure><noscript>&amp;lt;img src="https://pic2.zhimg.com/50/0a802fbc87cb675eba10a41f62f4b4fd_hd.png" data-rawwidth="600" data-rawheight="339" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="600" data-original="https://pic2.zhimg.com/0a802fbc87cb675eba10a41f62f4b4fd_r.png"&amp;gt;</noscript><span><div data-reactroot="" class="VagueImage origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" data-src="https://pic2.zhimg.com/50/0a802fbc87cb675eba10a41f62f4b4fd_hd.jpg" style="width: 600px; height: 339px;"><div class="VagueImage-mask is-active"></div></div></span></figure><p></p><p>看到这里，你会发现，这不仅仅是一个练手项目，而是一套专为初学者准备的、经过精心设计的系统课程。</p><ul><li>理解阶段：通过类比和课程案例，你能更轻松的掌握必要的知识。<br></li><li>模仿阶段：正如学习母语，小孩子通过模仿成人说话而记忆。模仿着课程里面的案例，去完成对应的练习题，能加深印象。<br></li><li>实战阶段：每个目标会对应一个大作业，同时也是课程项目的一部分。这时候你没办法再模仿着示例敲代码，而是需要独立解决问题，然后再去听大作业的讲解。经过自己的思考，再听课时你才会有这种感觉，「哇哦，我现在彻底明白了」，而不是「嗯，好像是这么回事」。<br></li></ul><br>有零基础的新手评价说：<br><blockquote>这是唯一能听懂的编程课，感觉和看美剧似的，会上瘾。</blockquote><br><p>他们身上，有了许多改变。</p><p>有一位同学，他是一名95年的大一学生，参加课程的目标是为了完成参加比赛的项目的内容爬取。<strong>而学习课程的第一周，他就达到了目标</strong>，参赛项目获得了四位数的奖金支持。</p><p>还有一位同学，他是一名产品经理，想为自己做一个时间管理的产品。在学习课程之前，还只停留在原型图阶段。而学习课程之后，拥有了亲手创造的能力，<strong>想法终于变成了现实</strong>。</p><p>正因为我们自己踩过这样的坑，面对一堆专业术语却看不懂的迷茫与挣扎、找了一堆资料却没有一个能把事说明白的痛苦与无奈。促使我们完成这门课程的最大动力是生气，生气怎么就没有一门符合初学者认知模式的科学体系，于是我们自己做了这门课。对了，它的名字叫：实战计划。</p><p>期待着为你带来改变。</p>免费一周课程：<a href="https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//study.163.com/course/introduction/1002810012.htm%23/courseDetail" class=" wrap external" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer">Python实战：一周学会爬取网页<i class="icon-external"></i></a><br>完整四周课程：<a href="https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//study.163.com/course/introduction/1002794001.htm%23/courseDetail" class=" wrap external" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer">Python实战：四周实现爬虫系统<i class="icon-external"></i></a></span><!-- react-empty: 2323 --></div><div><div class="ContentItem-time"><a target="_blank" href="/question/29372574/answer/86412439"><span data-tooltip="发布于 2016-02-15"><!-- react-text: 2328 -->编辑于 <!-- /react-text --><!-- react-text: 2329 -->2016-02-27<!-- /react-text
